Jane thanks the American Bar Association and President Bass for supporting the Law Library of Congress and its mission. Thank you for joining us for #LawDay.
Hilarie also says that with regard to the practice of law, technology will make us much more efficient and clients will demand that efficiency. Hilarie mentions outsourcing in document review as an example. #LawDay
Hilarie says that free online forms and other commercial providers are the tip of the iceberg for how law will change over the next 10 years to meet the demand of those who cannot afford a lawyer #LawDay
Jane asks Hilarie what the practice of law might look like in 10 years. Hilarie says it will look very different. First,  Hilarie says there is a huge justice gap, that 80% of Americans cannot afford a lawyer. #LawDay
Hilarie mentions ABA Legal Fact Check. She says they take a legal issue that has been in the news and provide non-partisan facts about that issue. #LawDay
Hilarie says she is focused on making the profession hospitable to diverse lawyers and transforming legal education to align it with what legal employers expect students to know when they graduate. #LawDay
Jane asks about Hilarie's time serving as the ABA President and asks her what she hopes her legacy will be.
Jane asks, what does separation of powers mean to the legal profession? Hilarie responds that the most important thing is supporting the independence of the judiciary by speaking out on its behalf. #LawDay
Hilarie says she is encouraged by the recent increase in engagement of younger people in American politics and their desire to participate in our democracy. #LawDay
Hilarie asks - how can you expect to maintain a democracy when 74% of citizens cannot identify the three branches of government? She says this issue underscores the importance of civics education. #LawDay
Jane asks Hilarie about the theme for #LawDay this year, ‚ÄúSeparation of Powers: Framework for Freedom.‚Äù Hilarie emphasizes the need for civics education in making Americans aware of the importance of the separation of powers and the importance of an independent judiciary.
Hilarie says she is very passionate about studying how to make a legal career more attractive for women and minorities. With regard to women in the profession, she mentions that we start out with law school classes that are 50% female, but many leave the profession later on.
Hilarie says she enjoyed political science and enjoyed political philosophy during college. After college she pursued her passion as an actress, acting in a soap opera. After the show ended, she decided to  attend law school. #LawDay
Jane asks Hilarie how she became a lawyer. #LawDay

Thank you for joining us for Mr. Signer's book talk on Becoming Madison. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - Madison referred to the people as the ultimate authority. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - Madison's optimism &amp; belief in statesmanship carried the day, defeating the anti-federalist opposition to the constitution.
Mr. Signer - Madison pushed back against some measure of nihilism on the part of the anti-federalists. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - The climax of the book is the ratifying convention and the rivalry between Patrick Henry and #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - Madison's opponents found his methods infuriating, inevitably dragging them to conclusions they did not want to make.
Mr. Signer - Madison's method of political advocacy employed many different arguments, rather than on focusing on finding a silver bullet.
Mr. Signer - One of Madison's methods of political advocacy focused on challenging ideas, not on attacking personalities.
Mr. Signer - Madison, contrary to popular perception, was not cold, calculating, and passionless. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer is troubled by the lack of discussion about the importance of statesmanship in the modern day. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - Becoming Madison is an intellectual and psychological biography of a young #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - The Federalist Papers explicitly addressed the challenge of the demagogue to democracy. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - the idea that demagogues will convert democracy into tyranny is grounded in the human condition itself. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer is discussing the challenge of the demagogue to democracy. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - This view of statesmanship is relevant to the modern day where our democratic institutions and practices are facing challenges.
Mr. Signer - leaders should seek to educate and challenge the public to embrace longterm, complex policies. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer - James Madison had many obstacles to his political success, not the least of which was he was shy. #JamesMadison
Mr. Signer is discussing Madison as an architect of statesmanship and his rivalry with Patrick Henry. #JamesMadison
